**OCP-23144**

To begin, Create remote cluster by running:<br/> export CLUSTER_NAME=&quot;qe-olnester&quot;<br/> export SSH_PUB_KEY=&quot;$(ssh-keygen -y -f ~/.ssh/libra.pem)&quot;<br/> export PULL_SECRET=&quot;$(cat ${HOME}/config.json)&quot;<br/> <br/> oc process -f config/templates/cluster-deployment.yaml \<br/> CLUSTER_NAME=&quot;${CLUSTER_NAME}&quot; \<br/> SSH_KEY=&quot;${SSH_PUB_KEY}&quot; \<br/> PULL_SECRET=&quot;${PULL_SECRET}&quot; \<br/> BASE_DOMAIN=qe.devcluster.openshift.com \<br/> AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID=&quot;${aws_access_key_id}&quot; \<br/> AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY=&quot;${aws_secret_access_key}&quot; \<br/> | oc apply -f -<br/>. then, Create template for configmap configmap.yaml:<br/> apiVersion: v1<br/> kind: ConfigMap<br/> metadata:<br/> name: foo<br/> namespace: default<br/> data:<br/> foo: bar<br/>. next, Go to the remote cluster and run <span style="font-weight: bold;">&quot;oc create configmap.yaml&quot;</span> and check results &quot;<span style="font-weight: bold;">oc get configmap -n default</span>&quot;<br/> — the expected outcome is: [onest@localhost go_openshift]$ oc get configmap -n default<br/> NAME DATA AGE<br/> foo 1 55s<br/>. after that, Go back to origin cluster and create syncset-patch.yaml template with :<br/> apiVersion: hive.openshift.io/v1<br/> kind: SyncSet<br/> metadata:<br/> name: test-patch<br/> spec:<br/> clusterDeploymentRefs:<br/> - name: testoleg<br/> patches:<br/> - kind: ConfigMap<br/> apiVersion: v1<br/> name: foo<br/> namespace: default<br/> patch: |-<br/> { &quot;data&quot;: { &quot;foo&quot;: &quot;new-bar&quot; } }<br/> patchType: merge<br/> <br/> and save changes<br/>. following this, Run &quot;<span style="font-weight: bold;">oc create -f syncset-patch.yaml</span>&quot;<br/> — the expected outcome is: [onest@localhost go_openshift]$ oc create -f syncset-patch.yaml<br/> syncset.hive.openshift.io/test-patch created<br/>. subsequently, Go to the remote cluster and check results: <span style="font-weight: bold;">&quot;oc get configmap foo -o yaml&quot;</span><br/> — the expected outcome is: [onest@localhost go_openshift]$ oc get configmap -o yaml<br/> apiVersion: v1<br/> items:<br/> - apiVersion: v1<br/> data:<br/> foo: <span style="font-weight: bold;">new-bar</span><br/> kind: ConfigMap<br/> metadata:<br/> creationTimestamp: 2019-04-11T14:58:09Z<br/> name: foo<br/> namespace: default<br/> resourceVersion: &quot;106779&quot;<br/> selfLink: /api/v1/namespaces/default/configmaps/foo3<br/> uid: 38a3b936-5c6a-11e9-87fc-0e9682aef3ce<br/> kind: List<br/> metadata:<br/> resourceVersion: &quot;&quot;<br/> selfLink: &quot;&quot;.

**OCP-23143**

To begin, Create cluster deployment <br/> export CLUSTER_NAME=&quot;<span style="font-weight: bold;">qe-olnester</span>&quot;<br/> export SSH_PUB_KEY=&quot;$(ssh-keygen -y -f ~/.ssh/libra.pem)&quot;<br/> export PULL_SECRET=&quot;$(cat ${HOME}/config.json)&quot;<br/> <br/> oc process -f config/templates/cluster-deployment.yaml \<br/> CLUSTER_NAME=&quot;${CLUSTER_NAME}&quot; \<br/> SSH_KEY=&quot;${SSH_PUB_KEY}&quot; \<br/> PULL_SECRET=&quot;${PULL_SECRET}&quot; \<br/> BASE_DOMAIN=qe.devcluster.openshift.com \<br/> AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID=&quot;${aws_access_key_id}&quot; \<br/> AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY=&quot;${aws_secret_access_key}&quot; \<br/> | oc apply -f -<br/>. then, Create syncset.yaml file template with the next data:<br/> [cloud-user@preserve-olnester-workstation 320]$ cat syncset.yaml <br/> apiVersion: hive.openshift.io/v1alpha1<br/> kind: SyncSet<br/> metadata:<br/> name: test-syncset<br/> spec:<br/> clusterDeploymentRefs:<br/> - name: oleg<br/> <span style="font-weight: bold;"> resourceApplyMode: &quot;Sync&quot;</span><br/> resources:<br/> - kind: ConfigMap<br/> apiVersion: v1<br/> metadata:<br/> name: foo1<br/> namespace: default<br/> data:<br/> foo: bar1<br/> <br/> - kind: ConfigMap<br/> apiVersion: v1<br/> metadata:<br/> name: foo2<br/> namespace: default<br/> data:<br/> foo: bar2<br/> <br/> <br/>. next, Run &quot;oc create -f syncset.yaml&quot; and check creation &quot;oc get syncset&quot;<br/> — the expected outcome is: <span style="font-weight: bold;"></span><span style="font-weight: normal;">[onest@localhost go_openshift]$ oc get syncset<br/> NAME AGE<br/> test-syncset 2m5s</span><span style="font-weight: bold;"></span>. after that, Login yo the remote cluster &quot;<span style="font-weight: bold;">qe-olnester</span>&quot; and go to the project &quot;default&quot;<br/>. following this, Run &quot;<span style="font-weight: bold;">oc get configmap</span>&quot;<br/> — the expected outcome is: oc [onest@localhost ~]$ oc get configmap<br/> NAME DATA AGE<br/> foo1 1 18s<br/> foo2 1 17s. subsequently, Edit syncset resource in origin cluster<br/> &quot;<span style="font-weight: bold;">oc edit syncset test-syncset</span>&quot;. continuing on, Delete next data:<br/> <span style="color: #FF0000;"> - kind: ConfigMap<br/> apiVersion: v1<br/> metadata:<br/> name: foo2<br/> namespace: default<br/> data:<br/> foo: bar2</span><br/> and save changes<br/>. moving forward, Go to the remote cluster and check results: run &quot;<span style="font-weight: bold;">oc get configmap&quot;</span><br/> — the expected outcome is: Confgimap &quot;foo2&quot; is deleted<br/> <br/> [onest@localhost ~]$ oc get configmap<br/> NAME DATA AGE<br/> foo1 1 11m<br/>.

---

**OCP-75241**

To begin, <span style="color: #000000;">1. **OCP-23986**

To begin, <span style="font-weight: normal;font-style: normal;text-decoration: none;font-size: 11pt;font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;color: #000000;line-height: 1.5;">Generate your own serving certificate and configure Hive to use it. Use the following instruction <a href="https://docs.google.com/document/d/19S1dA7ATXUos7dKZGtpnBiGidXhx--JX1lLgPgVj4Jo" target="_top" class="descriptionLink">https://docs.google.com/document/d/19S1dA7ATXUos7dKZGtpnBiGidXhx--JX1lLgPgVj4Jo</a> <br/> </span>. then, Download and install certbot for letsencrypt<br/> For instructions, go to <a href="https://certbot.eff.org/" style="color: #1155CC;">https://certbot.eff.org/</a> , pick ‘Others’ for the first dropdown and your OS for the second dropdown.<br/> <br/>. next, Create a directory on your local machine to hold the letsencrypt certificates and required subdirectories:<br/> <span style="font-size: 9pt;font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace;background-color: #EFEFEF;line-height: 1.5;">$ mkdir -p ~/letsencrypt/{config,logs,work}</span><br/> <br/>. after that, Create a new certificate for your cluster. For a 4.x cluster, you will need a certificate for the api endpoint and for the router wildcard.<br/> <span style="font-size: 9pt;font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace;background-color: #EFEFEF;line-height: 1.5;">$ cd ~/letsencrypt<br/> $ certbot certonly --config-dir ./config --work-dir ./work --logs-dir ./logs \<br/> --preferred-challenges dns --manual</span><br/> <br/> — the expected outcome is: [suyue@fedora ~]$ cd ~/letsencrypt<br/> <br/> <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">[suyue@fedora letsencrypt]$ certbot certonly --config-dir ./config --work-dir ./work --logs-dir ./logs --preferred-challenges dns --manual</span><br/> <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">Saving debug log to /home/suyue/letsencrypt/logs/letsencrypt.log</span><br/> <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">Enter email address (used for urgent renewal and security notices)</span><br/> <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;"> (Enter &#39;c&#39; to cancel): sguo@redhat.com</span><br/> <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;"><br/> </span><br/> <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - -</span><br/> <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">Please read the Terms of Service at</span><br/> <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">https://letsencrypt.org/documents/LE-SA-v1.3-September-21-2022.pdf. To renew this certificate, repeat this same certbot command before the certificate&#39;s expiry date.</span><br/> <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;"><br/> </span><br/> <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - -</span><br/> <br/>. following this, This shows how to add DNS record in the last step, you need to click the create record button<br/> <br/> use these two commands to check if the DNS record was created successfully.<br/> <br/> <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">dig _acme-challenge.apps.sguo-cert.qe.devcluster.openshift.com TXT<br/> dig _acme-challenge.api.sguo-cert.qe.devcluster.openshift.com TXT</span> — the expected outcome is: <img title="Screenshot from 2023-03-16 13-58-38.png" src="workitemimg:1-Screenshot_from_2023-03-16_13-58-38.png" style="max-width: 650px;"/>. subsequently, You can now create a secret for your serving certificate with oc:<br/> <span style="font-size: 8pt;font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace;background-color: #EFEFEF;line-height: 1.5;">oc create secret tls foo-serving-cert \<br/> --cert=$HOME/letsencrypt/config/live/api.foo.new-installer.openshift.com/fullchain.pem \<br/> --key=$HOME/letsencrypt/config/live/api.foo.new-installer.openshift.com/privkey.pem</span><br/> <br/> — the expected outcome is: [suyue@fedora letsencrypt]$ oc create secret tls foo-serving-cert --cert=/home/suyue/letsencrypt/config/live/api.sguo-cert.qe.devcluster.openshift.com/fullchain.pem --key=/home/suyue/letsencrypt/config/live/api.sguo-cert.qe.devcluster.openshift.com/privkey.pem<br/> secret/foo-serving-cert created<br/> <br/>. continuing on, <span style="font-size: 11pt;font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;line-height: 1.5;">One of the files that certbot creates when generating a new certificate is a chain.pem file (located in the same directory as the cert and private key files in step above. The chain.pem files contains a CA cert that can be used to validate certificates generated by letsencrypt. In order to configure it, first create a secret with it in the hive namespace:<br/> </span><span style="font-size: 8pt;font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace;background-color: #EFEFEF;line-height: 1.5;">$ oc create secret generic letsencrypt-ca -n hive --from-file=ca.crt=~/letsencrypt/config/live/api.foo.new-installer.openshift.com/chain.pem</span><br/> <span style="font-size: 11pt;font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;line-height: 1.5;">After creating the secret, edit hiveconfig with:<br/> </span><span style="font-size: 8pt;font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace;background-color: #EFEFEF;line-height: 1.5;">$ oc edit hiveconfig hive</span><br/> <span style="font-size: 11pt;font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;line-height: 1.5;">And add a reference to the secret in the config spec:<br/> </span><span style="font-size: 8pt;font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace;background-color: #EFEFEF;line-height: 1.5;">spec:</span><br/> <span style="font-size: 8pt;font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace;background-color: #EFEFEF;line-height: 1.5;"> additionalCertificateAuthorities:<br/> - name: letsencrypt-ca</span><br/> <br/> — the expected outcome is: [suyue@fedora letsencrypt]$ oc create secret generic letsencrypt-ca -n hive --from-file=ca.crt=$HOME/letsencrypt/config/live/api.sguo-cert.qe.devcluster.openshift.com/chain.pem<br/> secret/letsencrypt-ca created<br/> [suyue@fedora letsencrypt]$ oc edit hiveconfig hive<br/> hiveconfig.hive.openshift.io/hive edited<br/> <br/>. moving forward, <ol> <li>Generate a new clusterdeployment using hiveutil and save the yaml to a local file:<br/> <span style="font-size: 8pt;font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace;background-color: #EFEFEF;line-height: 1.5;">$ ./bin/hiveutil create-cluster foo --base-domain new-installer-openshift.com -o yaml &gt; /tmp/cluster.yaml</span><br/> </li> <li>Edit the clusterdeployment in /tmp/cluster.yaml by adding a certificate bundle entry under the clusterdeployment’s spec ( the name is arbitrary and is only used for reference within the clusterdeployment … in this case we’re using foocert, the secret ref must point to the secret you created in step 6 above:<br/> <span style="font-size: 8pt;font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace;background-color: #EFEFEF;line-height: 1.5;"> spec:<br/> certificateBundles:<br/> - name: foocert<br/> secretRef:<br/> name: foo-serving-cert</span><br/> </li> <li>Configure the control plane serving certs by editing controlPlaneConfig under spec and point to the certificate bundle defined in step 2:<br/> <span style="font-size: 9pt;font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace;background-color: #EFEFEF;line-height: 1.5;"> controlPlaneConfig:<br/> servingCertificates:<br/> default: foocert</span><br/> </li> <li>Configure the default ingress by adding an entry for the default ingress to the cluster deployment spec:<br/> <span style="font-size: 8pt;font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace;background-color: #EFEFEF;line-height: 1.5;"> spec:<br/> ingress:<br/> - name: default<br/> domain: apps.foo.new-installer.openshift.com<br/> servingCertificate: foocert</span><br/> </li> <li>Create the cluster with `oc apply`:<br/> <span style="font-size: 8pt;font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, Courier, monospace;background-color: #EFEFEF;line-height: 1.5;"> $ oc apply -f /tmp/cluster.yaml</span><br/> </li> </ol> — the expected outcome is: ........<br/> spec:<br/> baseDomain: qe.devcluster.openshift.com<br/> certificateBundles:<br/> - name: foocert<br/> certificateSecretRef:<br/> name: foo-serving-cert<br/> clusterName: sguo-cert<br/> controlPlaneConfig:<br/> servingCertificates:<br/> default: foocert<br/> ingress:<br/> - name: default<br/> domain: apps.sguo-cert.qe.devcluster.openshift.com<br/> servingCertificate: foocert<br/> .....<br/> <br/> [suyue@fedora hive]$ oc apply -f deployment.yaml <br/> clusterdeployment.hive.openshift.io/sguo-cert created<br/> machinepool.hive.openshift.io/sguo-cert-worker unchanged<br/> secret/sguo-cert-install-config configured<br/> secret/sguo-cert-pull-secret configured<br/> secret/sguo-cert-ssh-private-key configured<br/> secret/sguo-cert-aws-creds configured<br/> clusterimageset.hive.openshift.io/sguo-cert-imageset configured<br/> <br/> <br/> <br/> <br/>. proceeding further, <span style="font-size: 11pt;font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;line-height: 1.5;">Once the cluster finishes installing, it will apply the necessary configuration changes to the control plane and ingress so that the new certificates are in place. This may take a few minutes after installation is complete.</span><br/> <span style="font-size: 11pt;font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;line-height: 1.5;">You can validate that the new cluster’s control plane is configured with the letsencrypt certificates by curling its endpoint:<br/> <br/> $ curl -v <a href="https://api.foo.new-installer.openshift.com:6443" style="color: #1155CC;">https://api.foo.new-installer.openshift.com:6443</a></span><br/> <span style="font-size: 11pt;font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;line-height: 1.5;">You should not get any complaint from curl about not being able to validate the certificate and in the verbose output, you should see that the certificate has been signed by LetsEncrypt</span><br/> <span style="font-size: 11pt;font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;line-height: 1.5;">For the router certificate, you can simply go to the cluster’s console (URL should be in ClusterDeployment’s status). are OK). next, Configure with the proxy to Vsphere server and user_ca_bundle (Installer QE ca_bundle).<pre style="color: #1D1C1D;">jianpingshu@jshu-mac ~ % oc get proxy cluster -o yaml apiVersion: config.openshift.io/v1 kind: Proxy metadata: creationTimestamp: &quot;2023-04-20T02:53:30Z&quot; **OCP-50882**

To begin, 1.Extract the list of CredentialsRequest custom resources (CRs) from the OpenShift Container Platform release image(refer to <span class="polarion-rte-link" data-type="polarion" id="fake" data-custom-label="OCP-46768" data-url="/workitems?query=OCP-46768"></span> )<br/> $ mkdir credrequests<br/> $ oc -a ~/.pull-secret adm release extract --credentials-requests --cloud=alibabacloud --to=./credrequests $RELEASE_IMAGE<br/> — the expected outcome is: <span style="font-size: 11pt;color: #1D1C1D;line-height: 1.5;">ls ./credrequests</span><br style="color: #1D1C1D;"/> <span style="font-size: 11pt;color: #1D1C1D;line-height: 1.5;">0000_30_machine-api-operator_00_credentials-request.yaml 0000_50_cluster-ingress-operator_00-ingress-credentials-request.yaml</span><br style="color: #1D1C1D;"/> <span style="font-size: 11pt;color: #1D1C1D;line-height: 1.5;">0000_50_cluster-image-registry-operator_01-registry-credentials-request-alibaba.yaml 0000_50_cluster-storage-operator_03_credentials_request_alibaba.yaml</span>. then, 2. **OCP-23101**

To begin, <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">Deploy cluster and wait for finish:<br/> $export CLUSTER_NAME=&quot;qe-olegtest&quot;<br/> <br/> $ ./bin/hiveutil create-cluster ${CLUSTER_NAME} --base-domain qe1.devcluster.openshift.com -o yaml &gt; deployment.yaml<br/> <br/> $oc create -f deployment.yaml<br/> </span> — the expected outcome is: <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">secret/qe-olegtest-aws-creds created<br/> secret/qe-olegtest-pull-secret created<br/> secret/qe-olegtest-ssh-key created<br/> clusterdeployment.hive.openshift.io/qe-olegtest created<br/> </span>. then, <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">After installation, add an additional compute machineset &quot;infra&quot; to the cluster deployment<br/> <br/> $cat machinepool.yaml<br/> apiVersion: hive.openshift.io/v1<br/> kind: MachinePool<br/> metadata:<br/> name: lwan--hive-pro-0721-infra<br/> namespace: default<br/> spec:<br/> clusterDeploymentRef:<br/> name: lwan--hive-pro-0721<br/> name: infra<br/> platform:<br/> aws:<br/> rootVolume:<br/> iops: 100<br/> size: 22<br/> type: gp2<br/> type: m4.xlarge<br/> replicas: 1<br/> <br/> $oc create -f machinepool.yaml</span>. next, <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">Wait a few minutes, check machinesets and nodes created successfully on remote cluster, and machinesets has one replicas, nodes has only one created. Login to remote cluster,Run:<br/> $oc get machinesets-n openshift-machine-api<br/> $oc get nodes<br/> </span> — the expected outcome is: <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">[cloud-user@preserve-olnester-workstation hive]$ oc get nodes | grep worker<br/> <span style="font-weight: bold;">ip-10-0-138-192.us-east-2.compute.internal Ready worker 2m46s v1.13.4+1ad602308</span><br/> ip-10-0-138-219.us-east-2.compute.internal Ready worker 13m v1.13.4+1ad602308<br/> ip-10-0-148-79.us-east-2.compute.internal Ready worker 13m v1.13.4+1ad602308<br/> ip-10-0-163-82.us-east-2.compute.internal Ready worker 13m v1.13.4+1ad602308<br/> <br/> </span>. after that, <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">Check machineset has label &quot; hive.openshift.io/managed=true&quot;, run<br/> oc get machineset ${ms_name} -n openshift-machine-api -o json | jq -r &quot;.metadata.labels&quot;</span> — the expected outcome is: <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">$ oc get machineset -n openshift-machine-api lwan-hive-pro-0721-jtphc-worker-us-east-2a -o json | jq -r &quot;.metadata.labels&quot;<br/> {<br/> &quot;hive.openshift.io/machine-pool&quot;: &quot;worker&quot;,<br/> <span style="font-weight: bold;"> &quot;hive.openshift.io/managed&quot;: &quot;true&quot;,</span><br/> &quot;machine.openshift.io/cluster-api-cluster&quot;: &quot;lwan-hive-pro-0721-jtphc&quot;<br/> }<br/> <br/> </span>. following this, Modify machinepool .spec.replicas to 3 and save. Check modifying is successful, run:<br/> $oc edit machinepool lwanaz312-infra<br/> $oc get machinepool lwanaz312-infra -o yaml. subsequently, Wait a few minutes, check it was applied to remote cluster, Its scale to 3 machinesets and 3 nodes. Run:<br/> $oc get machinesets-n openshift-machine-api<br/> $oc get nodes. continuing on, Delete machinepool created above,run<br/> $oc delete machinepool lwanaz312-infra<br/> <br/> <br/> Check machinesets and nodes were deleted on remote cluster. Login to remote cluster,run<br/> $$oc get machinesets-n openshift-machine-api<br/> $oc get nodes.

**OCP-68240**

**OCP-29670**

To begin, <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">1.Install hive-operator<br/> <span style="text-decoration: line-through;">#way 1</span> (covered in OCP-29695)<span style="text-decoration: line-through;"><br/> #Login to cluster web console with kubeadmin user, and go to OperatorHub menu, filter by &quot;hive&quot;, click &quot;OpenShift Hive&quot;and enter.<br/> #Click the &quot;install&quot; button, then click &quot;Subscribe&quot;,and wait a minute</span><br/> #way 2<br/> # ./oc create ns hive<br/> namespace/hive created<br/> # cat og.yaml <br/> apiVersion: operators.coreos.com/v1<br/> kind: OperatorGroup<br/> metadata:<br/> name: hive-og<br/> namespace: hive<br/> spec:<br/> targetNamespaces:<br/> - hive<br/> # ./oc create -f og.yaml <br/> operatorgroup.operators.coreos.com/hive-og created<br/> # cat sub.yaml <br/> apiVersion: operators.coreos.com/v1alpha1<br/> kind: Subscription<br/> metadata:<br/> name: hive-sub<br/> namespace: hive<br/> spec:<br/> channel: alpha<br/> name: hive-operator<br/> approval: Automatic <br/> source: community-operators<br/> sourceNamespace: openshift-marketplace<br/> # ./oc create -f sub.yaml <br/> subscription.operators.coreos.com/hive-sub created</span> — the expected outcome is: <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;"> </span>. then, <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">2.Watch your operator come up,run:<br/> $oc get csv -n openshift-operators</span> — the expected outcome is: <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">$ oc get csv -n openshift-operators<br/> NAME DISPLAY VERSION REPLACES PHASE<br/> hive-operator.v1.0.1 OpenShift Hive 1.0.1 Succeeded<br/> </span>. next, <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">3.Verify the hive-operator is created in openshift-operators namespace,run<br/> $oc get pods -n openshift-operators</span> — the expected outcome is: <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">$ oc get pods -n openshift-operators<br/> NAME READY STATUS RESTARTS AGE<br/> hive-operator-697756c9c8-wrg9x 1/1 Running 0 90m<br/> </span>. after that, <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">4.Create a cluster-scoped HiveConfig CR to configure hive, <span style="text-decoration: line-through;">move to &quot;Installed Operators-&gt;OpenShift Hive-&gt;Hive Config&quot;, and click &quot;Create Hive Config&quot; button, and put the below text to it and click &quot;Create&quot;</span><br/> </span><pre style="color: #363636;"><code>apiVersion: hive.openshift.io/v1 kind: HiveConfig metadata: name: hive spec: logLevel: debug<br/> targetNamespace: hive</code></pre> — the expected outcome is: <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;"><img title="1-2020-04-17_12-41-32_的屏幕截图.png" src="workitemimg:1-2020-04-17_12-41-32_%E7%9A%84%E5%B1%8F%E5%B9%95%E6%88%AA%E5%9B%BE.png" style="max-width: 750px;"/><br/> <br/> </span>. following this, <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">5.Verify Hive&#39;s pods are created in hive namespace,run,<br/> $oc get pods -n hive</span> — the expected outcome is: <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">$ oc get pods -n hive<br/> NAME READY STATUS RESTARTS AGE<br/> hive-controllers-667bbf8b99-wqjpt 1/1 Running 0 72m<br/> hiveadmission-5d65dcb7b9-f8s28 1/1 Running 0 72m<br/> hiveadmission-5d65dcb7b9-r85sz 1/1 Running 0 72m<br/> <br/> </span>. subsequently, 6. <span style="font-size: 9pt;font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;, Times, serif;line-height: 1.5;">Verify if you are able to see the log message in the below format</span><br/> $ <span style="font-size: 9pt;line-height: 1.5;">oc logs -n hive hiveadmission-5d65dc7b9-r85sz | head -1</span> — the expected outcome is: <span style="font-size: 9pt;font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;, Times, serif;line-height: 1.5;">$ oc logs -n hive hiveadmission-5d65dc7b9-r85sz | head -1<br/> time=&quot;2022-05-10T18:52:16Z&quot; level=info msg=&quot;Version: openshift/hive v1.2.3633-595563c&quot;</span>.

**OCP-28631**

To begin, <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">1. Deploy a clusterdeployment,run :<br/> $./bin/hiveutil create-cluster lwan --base-domain qe.devcluster.openshift.com --release-image registry.svc.ci.openshift.org/ocp/release:4.5.0-0.nightly-2020-03-10-002435</span>. then, <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">2.Wait until clusterdeployment was created and has infraid,run:<br/> $oc get cd</span> — the expected outcome is: <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">$ oc get cd<br/> NAME CLUSTERNAME CLUSTERTYPE BASEDOMAIN INSTALLED INFRAID AGE<br/> lwanqe lwanqe qe.devcluster.openshift.com false <span style="font-weight: bold;">lwanqe-nn8tc</span> 83s<br/> <br/> </span>. next, <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">3. Disable deprovision through a hiveconfig option,run:<br/> $oc ecit hiveconfig hive<br/> Then set spec.deprovisionsDisabled = &quot;true&quot; and save</span> — the expected outcome is: <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">$ oc edit hiveconfig hive<br/> hiveconfig.hive.openshift.io/hive edited<br/> <br/> </span>. after that, <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">4. Check modified is successful,Run:<br/> $oc get hiveconfig hive -o yaml</span> — the expected outcome is: <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">$ oc get hiveconfig hive -o yaml<br/> apiVersion: hive.openshift.io/v1<br/> kind: HiveConfig<br/> metadata:<br/> creationTimestamp: &quot;2020-03-10T04:40:12Z&quot;<br/> generation: 2<br/> name: hive<br/> resourceVersion: &quot;156512&quot;<br/> selfLink: /apis/hive.openshift.io/v1/hiveconfigs/hive<br/> uid: bb46397f-383d-4a68-8022-29fd7d1f69d8<br/> spec:<br/> backup:<br/> velero: {}<br/> <span style="font-weight: bold;">deprovisionsDisabled: true</span><br/> failedProvisionConfig: {}<br/> status:<br/> aggregatorClientCAHash: 67aa8a24d90b3b77254051191c17456b<br/> configApplied: true<br/> observedGeneration: 2</span>. following this, <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">5. Delete clusterdeployment just created,and check no uninstall pod is created<br/> $oc delete cd cluster<br/> $oc get pods</span> — the expected outcome is: <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">$oc delete cd cluster<br/> $ oc get pods<br/> NAME READY STATUS RESTARTS AGE<br/> hive-controllers-f8f5d955c-f8k44 1/1 Running 0 7m40s<br/> hive-operator-7b7f6fc44d-5wzm9 1/1 Running 0 6h44m<br/> hiveadmission-76c4f785d5-f2txv 1/1 Running 0 32m<br/> hiveadmission-76c4f785d5-pw72w 1/1 Running 0 33m<br/> </span>. subsequently, <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">6.Check logs of hive-controller has a warning :&quot;deprovisions are currently disabled in HiveConfig, skipping&quot;.Run:<br/> $oc logs deployment/hive-controllers | grep deprovisions</span> — the expected outcome is: <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">$ oc logs deployment/hive-controllers | grep deprovisions<br/> time=&quot;2020-03-10T11:17:30Z&quot; level=warning msg=&quot;deprovisions are currently disabled in HiveConfig, skipping&quot; controller=clusterDeprovision name=hive/lwanqe<br/> </span>. continuing on, <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">7.Edit the hiveconfig again and set the field to false, then check modified is successful,run:<br/> $oc edit hiveconfig hive<br/> $oc get hiveconfig hive -o yaml<br/> </span> — the expected outcome is: <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">$ oc get hiveconfig hive -o yaml<br/> apiVersion: hive.openshift.io/v1<br/> kind: HiveConfig<br/> metadata:<br/> creationTimestamp: &quot;2020-03-10T04:40:12Z&quot;<br/> generation: 2<br/> name: hive<br/> resourceVersion: &quot;156512&quot;<br/> selfLink: /apis/hive.openshift.io/v1/hiveconfigs/hive<br/> uid: bb46397f-383d-4a68-8022-29fd7d1f69d8<br/> spec:<br/> backup:<br/> velero: {}<br/> <span style="font-weight: bold;">deprovisionsDisabled: false</span><br/> failedProvisionConfig: {}<br/> status:<br/> aggregatorClientCAHash: 67aa8a24d90b3b77254051191c17456b<br/> configApplied: true<br/> observedGeneration: 2</span>. moving forward, <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">8.wait several minutes,and check uninstall job kick off.run:<br/> $oc get pods</span> — the expected outcome is: <span style="font-size: 10pt;line-height: 1.5;">[linwang@localhost hive]$ oc get pods<br/> NAME READY STATUS RESTARTS AGE<br/> hive-controllers-f8f5d955c-f8k44 1/1 Running 0 15m<br/> hive-operator-7b7f6fc44d-5wzm9 1/1 Running 0 6h52m<br/> hiveadmission-76c4f785d5-f2txv 1/1 Running 0 40m<br/> hiveadmission-76c4f785d5-pw72w 1/1 Running 0 40m<br/> <span style="font-weight: bold;">lwanqe-uninstall-lb4w9 </span> 1/1 Running 0 18m<br/> <br/> </span>.

**OCP-25310**

To begin, Deploy hive<br/>. then, Create clusterdeployment:<br/> $ ./bin/hiveutil create-cluster fxie-hive-1 --base-domain qe.devcluster.openshift.com --cloud aws --ssh-public-key-file ~/.ssh/ocp_ed25519_2.pub --region us-east-2<br/> <br/> and wait cluster is installed<br/>. next, Run <span style="font-weight: bold;">oc get clusterdeployment olegtest -o yaml or<br/> oc get cd olegtest -o json | jq &#39;.spec .installed&#39;<br/> </span> — the expected outcome is: Make sure that ClusterDeployment.spec.installed = true<br/> <br/> [onest@localhost hive]$ oc get cd olegtest -o yaml<br/> apiVersion: hive.openshift.io/v1alpha1<br/> kind: ClusterDeployment<br/> metadata:<br/> annotations:<br/> ........<br/> spec:<br/> baseDomain: hive.openshift.com<br/> clusterName: olegtest<br/> compute:<br/> - name: worker<br/> ....<br/> controlPlaneConfig:<br/> servingCertificates: {}<br/> imageSet:<br/> name: openshift-v4.0-latest<br/> images:<br/> installerImagePullPolicy: Always<br/> releaseImage: registry.svc.ci.openshift.org/ocp/release:4.2.0-0.nightly-2019-09-20-040328<br/> <span style="font-weight: bold;"> installed: true</span><br/> networking:<br/> clusterNetworks:<br/> - cidr: 10.128.0.0/14<br/> hostSubnetLength: 23<br/> machineCIDR: 10.0.0.0/16<br/> serviceCIDR: 172.30.0.0/16<br/> type: OpenShiftSDN<br/> platform:<br/> aws:<br/> region: us-east-1<br/> platformSecrets:<br/> aws:<br/> credentials:<br/> name: olegtest-aws-creds<br/> pullSecret:<br/> name: olegtest-pull-secret<br/> sshKey:<br/> name: olegtest-ssh-key<br/> .......<br/> <br/> [onest@localhost hive]$ oc get cd olegtest -o json | jq &#39;.spec .installed&#39;<br/> true<br/>.
